<userid>111386976746251152243</userid><user_name>Lisi Lewis<//user_name><time>1597518969432</time>< rating>

< review>
**AVOID THIS COMPANY AT ALL COSTS**

Our items were picked up from Laguna Beach, California on July 13th for a cross country move to Sarasota, Florida. The move was sub-contracted to someone who, after picking all of our stuff up, informed us that 8 of our boxes were left behind in a warehouse somewhere in California -- the exact location was not disclosed.

My husband and I have called and emailed Allied over 15 times trying to get information on the location and status of our remaining items. On July 28th, we finally got a response from someone saying they were on a truck across the country, but no more information.

Yesterday, I followed up again and was told the items were getting on a truck yesterday (not on the 28th, like they said they were). I have completely lost confidence that anyone knows where our items are and when they're going to arrive.

There are over $10,000 in items that are missing, including our silverware from our wedding, pots, pans, a television, a grill, smaller kitchen appliances like our mixer, toaster, etc. We have had to purchase some replacement items because these items are things we need to use on a day-to-day basis.

Additionally, many of the items that actually were delivered are damaged. Our headboard has a few chunks taken out from it, our side table is scratched to hell, and the movers took a huge chunk of the wood floor out upon moving into our rental, which we'll definitely be charged for upon our move out.

< Review>
Unprofessional Organization.  Unfortunately, on-line reviews don't truly represent the experience you may have or the risk of avoiding significant stress and frustration!  So, ask many questions and read the fine print in the agreement.  I chose Berger because of their customer reviews and I still received terrible service and results from a full truckload move between California and Utah.  I will try to be concise and stick to the facts to help other families looking to move and choose a moving partner.  Bottomline, I moved 11 hours away by car, yet received my personal property 13 days later by train!  The Berger agents (including Teanna Herd Berger coordinator) actually stated they didn't know it was shipping by train and also couldn't tell me where my items were until a day before they arrived!  Further, they charged me a premium rate for delivery over the July 4th week, and missed the guarantee delivery date anyway.  Yet, they expected me to fill out a late claim that limited their exposure to only actual expenses and less than what I had to pay them in premium cost.  Finally, every individual including Troy Amidon (Berger sales), Greg Maher (Berger GM), and Samantha Fisher (Sirva-Worldwide Customer Agent) all stated they did not have the authority to reverse the train shipping decision or credit me for the additional rate paid.  In fact, the Berger agents said even though I reserved a move 2 months in advance with them, they had no responsibility in reserving a truck and in putting my items on a train.  They said that was Allied Corporate.  This is very unprofessional and feels like they oversold to lock up the premium rates and deliveries, or worse they didn't manage the details of the agreements they signed.  I'm still waiting 2 weeks later for someone who has the authority to address my complaint of the cost and overall terrible customer experience.  I have much more details to share that are negative examples of my experience.  But, let me just end by saying that I wished I would have gone with another national moving company that quoted me lower and didn't have misleading on-line positive reviews.  Lesson learned for me is that with moving companies like Berger/Allied, customer success is not a priority and you can't always trust customer reviews.  So, focus on cost and try to transport your most valuable items yourself.  By the way, I also have damage claims to still file and the movers who unloaded took no responsibility for how items were loaded by someone else at Allied.  The entire Berger/Allied Team left me disappointed, frustrated, and even angry.  This is my first ever negative review I posted about a Company.  Good luck and I wish you all better moving results!<//Review>

<rate>5< /rate>< UserId.>
109499394982496437937</UserId.>
<pics>None<//pics><Time>1546124113684< /Time>< text>
Short Review: great place for families.

Long Review: know the rules and know that they will not bend or break them for you... liability issues.

As of summer 2018 it was $1 for kids $3.50 for adults. No more discounts with a library card. Everyone entering the pool must have swimwear. No white tops and shorts must have inner lining. No jeans/jean shorts, basketball, soccer, leggings... must be swimwear. Babies/Toddlers must wear swim diapers. Anyone under the age of 7 must have an adult within hands distance at all times with a 1 on 1 ratio. That means one adult per child under 7.

Hours of operation and opening/closing days vary due to funding. In summer 2018 the pool was open one month longer on weekends only. Do not go by the hours posted on google. Anyone can get on and change the hours with false information. Call their office to get the right information. Do not call the recreation's office as they don't always get the information (2 different departments, Recreation & Aquatics).

There is street parking (read the signs) but street cleaning and permit parking limits parking on Thursdays and Fridays. The parking lot can fill up quick with patrons and people who are cheap and don't want to pay $0.50 to park at their gym.

There is no shady area or a place to have lunch/picnic in the pool area. Reason is to keep the area as clean as possible and not mess with the filtration system. If you want to have lunch/picnic, there are plenty of areas within the park. Note, summer lunch program uses the picnic area to distribute lunches from 12pm-12:45pm and only kids are allowed in that area.

I hope this helps people so they're not surprised when they visit. If you have any questions, call the office when they open summer 2019. It's usually when LAUSD is on summer break. You're looking at early June to mid August.< /text>

1571702429667<//Time>
< Rating>
4< /Rating>
< text>
Sonic has more variety than most fast food places, and they've tried to capture, to some extent, the nostalgic feeling some of us old-timers remember from the drive-ins we used to go to. The high-tech ordering stations flanking each parking space can be intimidating the first time you try to use them, however.  For those who have less time on their hands, they also offer drive-thru service. Their prices are pretty reasonable, as fast food goes.  But a "famous root beer stand" they are not.</text>
